else if ([Registration][F03-Registration request][CRACONF][REQSTATUS]==1 && [Registration][F03-Registration request][REQCC][FCHECK] ==0){

if ([Registration][F03-Registration request][REQCC][CHECKREQ]=='0') com = com + "-on this form (Inclusion request);";
}

else if ([Registration][F03-Registration request][CRACONF][REQSTATUS]==2 && [Registration][F03-Registration request][REQCC][FCHECK] ==1){
com=' No Protocol(s) deviation(s) detected';}
}

### Cancer diagnosis 

<table style='width:100%;'>

<td style='width:50px; text-align:center; color:red; font-size: 10px;'> <b> DIAGDT </b></td> 
 <td style='width:600px; text-align:left;'> Date of tumor diagnosis</td>
 <td style='width:600px; text-align:left;'>  <details> <summary>2 EditCheck </summary><table><tr><td> Valid:[Patient Template][Baseline.*][F08-LCD.*][Cancer diagnosis.*][DIAGDT]</td> </tr><tr> <td> <pre><code class='javascript'>#Action Expression

 <tr> 
<td style='width:50px; text-align:center; color:red; font-size: 10px;'> <b> ðŸ”’Flags </b></td> 
 <td style='width:600px; text-align:left;'> Result</td>
 <td style='width:600px; text-align:left;'>  <details> <summary>2 EditCheck </summary><table><tr><td> Enabled:[Lab Normal Tests.*][Flags]</td> </tr><tr> <td> <pre><code class='javascript'>#Action Expression 
!isEmpty([Lab Normal Tests][LabTestR]) ; 
#data Expression 
 
</code></pre> </td><td> </td> </tr><tr><td> DVA:[F11-LB.*][Lab Normal Tests.*][Flags]</td> </tr><tr> <td> <pre><code class='javascript'>#Action Expression 
!isEmpty([F11-LB][Lab Normal Tests][LabTestR]) &&
!isEmpty([F11-LB][Lab Normal Tests][LabMin]) &&
!isEmpty([F11-LB][Lab Normal Tests][LabMax]); 
#data Expression 
var labmin = Number([F11-LB][Lab Normal Tests][LabMin]);
var labmax = Number([F11-LB][Lab Normal Tests][LabMax]);
var res = Number([F11-LB][Lab Normal Tests][LabTestR]);

if (res < labmin) 'Low';
else if (res > labmax) 'High';
else if ((res >= labmin) && (res <= labmax)) 'Normal' ; 
</code></pre> </td><td> </td> </tr></table></details> </td>
 <td style='width:300px; text-align:center;'> Char - 6 </td> 
 </tr>
 <tr> 
<td style='width:50px; text-align:center; color:red; font-size: 10px;'> <b> ðŸ”’Grade </b></td> 
 <td style='width:600px; text-align:left;'> Grade</td>
 <td style='width:600px; text-align:left;'>  <details> <summary>2 EditCheck </summary><table><tr><td> Enabled:[Lab Normal Tests.*][Grade]</td> </tr><tr> <td> <pre><code class='javascript'>#Action Expression 
!isEmpty([Lab Normal Tests.@][LabTestR]) ; 
#data Expression 
 
</code></pre> </td><td> </td> </tr><tr><td> DVA:[Lab Normal Tests.*][Grade]</td> </tr><tr> <td> <pre><code class='javascript'>#Action Expression 
false; 
#data Expression 
var grade = [Lab Normal Tests][Grade];
var lln = Number([Lab Normal Tests][LabMin]);
var uln = Number([Lab Normal Tests][LabMax]);
var res = Number([Lab Normal Tests][LabTestR]);
var test = [Lab Normal Tests][LabTestN];
var clinic = [Lab Normal Tests][BIOSPE];

// WHITE BLOOD CELLS
    // White blood cell decreased
if (test == 'White blood cells'){
if (res < 1) grade = 4;
if (res >= 1 && res < 2) grade = 3;
if (res >= 2 && res < 3) grade = 2;
if (res >= 3 && res < lln) grade = 1;
if (res >= lln && res <= uln) grade = 0;
if (res > uln) grade = 'NA'; };


// HEMOGLOBIN
if (test == 'Hemoglobin'){
if (res >= lln && res <= uln) grade = 0;
   // Anemia
if (clinic=='4' || clinic=='8') grade = 4;
if ((res < 8 && clinic=='') || clinic=='2') grade = 3;
if (res >= 8 && res < 10 && clinic=='') grade = 2;
if (res >= 10 && res < lln && clinic=='') grade = 1;
   // Hemoglobin increased
if (res > uln && res <= (uln+2)) grade = 1;
if (res > (uln+2) && res <= (uln+4)) grade = 2;
if (res > (uln+4)) grade = 3;
if (isEmpty(uln) && isEmpty(lln)) grade = 'NA'};

// PLATELETS
    // Platelet count decreased
if (test == 'Platelets'){
if (res < 25) grade = 4;
if (res >= 25 && res < 50) grade = 3;
if (res >= 50 && res < 75) grade = 2;
if (res >= 75 && res < lln) grade = 1;
if (res >= lln && res <= uln) grade = 0;
if (res > uln) grade = 'NA';};

// NEUTROPHILS
    // Neutrophil count decreased
if (test == 'Neutrophils'){
if (res < 0.5) grade = 4;
if (res >= 0.5 && res < 1) grade = 3;
if (res >= 1 && res < 1.5) grade = 2;
if (res >= 1.5 && res < lln) grade = 1;
if (res >= lln && res <= uln) grade = 0;
if (res > uln) grade = 'NA';};


// EOSINOPHILS
if (test == 'Eosinophils') grade = 'NA';


// BASOPHILS
if (test == 'Basophils') grade = 'NA';


// LYMPHOCYTES
if (test == 'Lymphocytes'){
if (res >= lln && res <= uln) grade = 0;
    // Lymphocyte count decreased
if (res < 0.2) grade = 4;
if (res >= 0.2 && res < 0.5) grade = 3;
if (res >= 0.5 && res < 0.8) grade = 2;
if (res >= 0.8 && res < lln) grade = 1;
    // Lymphocyte count increased
if (res > 4 && res <= 20) grade = 2;
if (res > 20) grade = 3;
if (isEmpty(uln) && isEmpty(lln)) grade = 'NA'};


// MONOCYTES
if (test == 'Monocytes') grade = 'NA';


// SODIUM
if (test == 'Sodium'){
if (res >= lln && res <= uln) grade = 0;
    // Hyponatremia
if ((res < 120 && clinic=='') || clinic=='8') grade = 4;
if (res >= 120 && res < 130 && clinic=='') grade = 3;
if (res >= 130 && res < lln && clinic=='') grade = 1;
    // Hypernatremia
if ((res > 160 && clinic=='') || clinic=='8') grade = 4;
if ((res > 155 && res <= 160 && clinic=='') || clinic=='3') grade = 3;
if (res > 150 && res <= 155 && clinic=='') grade = 2;
if (res > uln && res <= 150 && clinic=='') grade = 1;
if (isEmpty(uln) && isEmpty(lln) && isEmpty(clinic)) grade = 'NA'};


// POTASSIUM
if (test == 'Potassium'){
if (res >= lln && res <= uln) grade = 0;
    // Hypokalemia
if ((res < 2.5 && clinic=='') || clinic=='8') grade = 4;
if ((res >= 2.5 && res < 3 && clinic=='') || clinic=='3') grade = 3;
if (clinic=='1' || clinic=='4') grade = 2;
if (res >= 3 && res < lln && clinic=='') grade = 1;
    // Hyperkalemia
if ((res > 7 && clinic=='') || clinic=='8') grade = 4;
if ((res > 6 && res <= 7 && clinic=='') || clinic=='3') grade = 3;
if (res > 5.5 && res <= 6 && clinic=='') grade = 2;
if (res > uln && res <= 5.5 && clinic=='') grade = 1;
if (isEmpty(uln) && isEmpty(lln)) grade = 'NA'};


// CHLORIDE
if (test == 'Chloride') grade = 'NA';


// GLUCOSE
if (test == 'Glucose'){
if (res >= lln && res <= uln) grade = 0;
    // Hypoglycemia
if ((res < 1.7) || clinic=='8' || clinic=='7') grade = 4;
if (res >= 1.7 && res < 2.2 && clinic=='') grade = 3;
if (res >= 2.2 && res < 3 && clinic=='') grade = 2;
if (res >= 3 && res < lln && clinic=='') grade = 1;
    // Hyperglycemia
if (res > 27.8 || clinic=='8') grade = 4;
if ((res > 13.9 && res <= 27.8 && clinic=='') || clinic=='3') grade = 3;
if (res > 8.9 && res <= 13.9 && clinic=='') grade = 2;
if (res > uln && res <= 8.9 && clinic=='') grade = 1;
if (isEmpty(uln) && isEmpty(lln) && isEmpty(clinic)) grade = 'NA'};


// CALCIUM
if (test == 'Calcium'){
if (res >= lln && res <= uln) grade = 0;
    // Hypocalcemia
if ((res < 1.5) || clinic=='8') grade = 4; 
if ((res >= 1.5 && res < 1.75 && clinic=='') || clinic=='3') grade = 3;
if ((res >= 1.75 && res < 2 && clinic=='') || clinic=='1') grade = 2;
if (res >= 2 && res < lln && clinic=='') grade = 1;
    // Hypercalcemia
if ((res > 3.4) || clinic=='8') grade = 4;
if ((res > 3.1 && res <= 3.4 && clinic=='') || clinic=='3') grade = 3;
if ((res > 2.9 && res <= 3.1 && clinic=='') || clinic=='1') grade = 2;
if (res > uln && res <= 2.9 && clinic=='') grade = 1;
if (isEmpty(uln) && isEmpty(lln) && isEmpty(clinic)) grade = 'NA'};


// PHOSPHORUS
if (test == 'Phosphorus') grade = 'NA';


// URIC ACID
    // Hyperuricemia
if (test == 'Uric acid'){
if (res > 590 || clinic=='8') grade = 4;
if (res > uln && res <= 590 && clinic=='6') grade = 3;
if (res > uln && res <= 590 && clinic=='5') grade = 1;
if (res < lln) grade = 'NA';
if (isEmpty(uln) && isEmpty(lln)) grade = 'NA'};


// MAGNESIUM
if (test == 'Magnesium'){
if (res >= lln && res <= uln) grade = 0;
    // Hypomagnesemia
if (res < 0.3 || clinic=='8') grade = 4;
if (res >= 0.3 && res < 0.4 && clinic=='') grade = 3;
if (res >= 0.4 && res < 0.5 && clinic=='') grade = 2;
if (res >= 0.5 && res < lln && clinic=='') grade = 1;
    // Hypermagnesemia
if (res > 3.3 || clinic=='8') grade = 4;
if (res > 1.23 && res <= 3.3 && clinic=='') grade = 3;
if (res > uln && res <= 1.23 && clinic=='') grade = 1;
if (isEmpty(uln) && isEmpty(lln) && isEmpty(clinic)) grade = 'NA'};


// ALKALINE PHOSPHATASE (PAL)
if (test == 'Alkaline phosphatase'){
if (res >= lln && res <= uln) grade = 0;
if (res < lln) grade = 'NA';
    // Alkaline phosphatase increased
if (res > (20*uln)) grade = 4;
if (res > (5*uln) && res <= (20*uln)) grade = 3;
if (res > (2.5*uln) && res <= (5*uln)) grade = 2;
if (res > uln && res <= (2.5*uln)) grade = 1;
if (isEmpty(uln) && isEmpty(lln)) grade = 'NA'};


// ASPARTATE AMINOTRANSFERASE (ASAT)
if (test == 'Aspartate aminotransferase (ASAT)'){
if (res >= lln && res <= uln) grade = 0;
if (res < lln) grade = 'NA';
    // Aspartate aminotransferase increased
if (res > (20*uln)) grade = 4;
if (res > (5*uln) && res <= (20*uln)) grade = 3;
if (res > (3*uln) && res <= (5*uln)) grade = 2;
if (res > uln && res <= (3*uln)) grade = 1;
if (isEmpty(uln) && isEmpty(lln)) grade = 'NA'};


// ALANINE AMINOTRANSFERASE (ALAT]
if (test == 'Alanine aminotransferase (ALAT)'){
if (res >= lln && res <= uln) grade = 0;
if (res < lln) grade = 'NA';
    // Alanine aminotransferase increased
if (res > (20*uln)) grade = 4;
if (res > (5*uln) && res <= (20*uln)) grade = 3;
if (res > (3*uln) && res <= (5*uln)) grade = 2;
if (res > uln && res <= (3*uln)) grade = 1;
if (isEmpty(uln) && isEmpty(lln)) grade = 'NA'};


// TOTAL BILIRUBIN
if (test == 'Total bilirubin'){
if (res >= lln && res <= uln) grade = 0;
if (res < lln) grade = 'NA';
    // Blood bilirubin increased
if (res > (10*uln)) grade = 4;
if (res > (3*uln) && res <=(10*uln)) grade = 3;
if (res > (1.5*uln) && res <= (3*uln)) grade = 2;
if (res > uln && res <= (1.5*uln)) grade = 1
if (isEmpty(uln) && isEmpty(lln)) grade = 'NA'};


// ALBUMIN
if (test == 'Albumin'){
if (res >= lln && res <= uln) grade = 0;
if (res > uln) grade = 'NA';
    // Hypoalbuminemia
if (res < lln && clinic=='8') grade = 4;
if (res < 20 && clinic=='') grade = 3;
if (res >= 20 && res < 30 && clinic=='') grade = 2;
if (res >= 30 && res < lln && clinic=='') grade = 1;};


// LACTATE DESHYDROGENASE (LDH)
if (test == 'Lactate deshydrogenase (LDH)') grade = 'NA';


// TOTAL PROTEIN
if (test == 'Total protein') grade = 'NA';


// PT (INR)
if (test == 'PT (INR)'){
if (res >= lln && res <= uln) grade = 0;
if (res < lln) grade = 'NA';
    // INR increased
if (res > (2.5*uln)) grade = 3;
if (res > (1.5*uln) && res <= (2.5*uln)) grade = 2;
if (res > uln && res <= (1.5*uln)) grade = 1;
if (isEmpty(uln) && isEmpty(lln)) grade = 'NA'};


// ACTIVATED PARTIAL THROMBOPLASTIN TIME
if (test == 'aPTT'){
if (res >= lln && res <= uln) grade = 0;
if (res < lln) grade = 'NA';
    // Activated partial thromboplastin time prolonged
if ((res > (2.5*uln)) || clinic=='9') grade = 3;
if (res > (1.5*uln) && res <= (2.5*uln) && clinic=='') grade = 2;
if (res > uln && res <= (1.5*uln) && clinic=='') grade = 1;
if (isEmpty(uln) && isEmpty(lln) && isEmpty(clinic)) grade = 'NA'};


// TOTAL TRIIODOTHYRONINE (T3)
if (test == 'Free triiodothyronine (FT3)') grade = 'NA';


// FREE TYROXINE (T4)
if (test == 'Free tyroxine (FT4)') grade = 'NA';


// THYROID STIMULATING HORMONE (TSH)
if (test == 'Thyroid stimulating hormone (TSH)') grade = 'NA';

// CREATININE
if (test == 'Creatinine'){
if (res >= lln && res <= uln) grade = 0;
if (res < lln) grade = 'NA';
    // Creatinine increased
if (res > (6*uln)) grade = 4;
if (res > (3*uln) && res <=(6*uln)) grade = 3;
if (res > (1.5*uln) && res <= (3*uln)) grade = 2;
if (res > uln && res <= (1.5*uln)) grade = 1;
if (isEmpty(uln) && isEmpty(lln)) grade = 'NA'};

// CREATININE CLEARANCE)
if (test == 'Creatinine clearance (mesured or calculated)') grade = 'NA';

// BLOOD UREA NITROGEN
if (test == 'Blood urea nitrogen') grade = 'NA' ;
else "";

var labmax = Number([F11-LB][Lab Normal Tests][LabMax]);
var res = Number([F11-LB][Lab Normal Tests][LabTestR]);

if (res < labmin) 'Low';
else if (res > labmax) 'High';
else if ((res >= labmin) && (res <= labmax)) 'Normal' ;

 <tr> 
<td style='width:50px; text-align:center; color:red; font-size: 10px;'> <b> ðŸ”’Grade </b></td> 
 <td style='width:600px; text-align:left;'> Grade</td>
 <td style='width:600px; text-align:left;'>  <details> <summary>2 EditCheck </summary><table><tr><td> Enabled:[Lab Normal Tests.*][Grade]</td> </tr><tr> <td> <pre><code class='javascript'>#Action Expression 
!isEmpty([Lab Normal Tests.@][LabTestR]) ; 
#data Expression 
 
</code></pre> </td><td> </td> </tr><tr><td> DVA:[Lab Normal Tests.*][Grade]</td> </tr><tr> <td> <pre><code class='javascript'>#Action Expression 
false; 
#data Expression 
var grade = [Lab Normal Tests][Grade];
var lln = Number([Lab Normal Tests][LabMin]);
var uln = Number([Lab Normal Tests][LabMax]);
var res = Number([Lab Normal Tests][LabTestR]);
var test = [Lab Normal Tests][LabTestN];
var clinic = [Lab Normal Tests][BIOSPE];

// WHITE BLOOD CELLS
    // White blood cell decreased
if (test == 'White blood cells'){
if (res < 1) grade = 4;
if (res >= 1 && res < 2) grade = 3;
if (res >= 2 && res < 3) grade = 2;
if (res >= 3 && res < lln) grade = 1;
if (res >= lln && res <= uln) grade = 0;
if (res > uln) grade = 'NA'; };


// HEMOGLOBIN
if (test == 'Hemoglobin'){
if (res >= lln && res <= uln) grade = 0;
   // Anemia
if (clinic=='4' || clinic=='8') grade = 4;
if ((res < 8 && clinic=='') || clinic=='2') grade = 3;
if (res >= 8 && res < 10 && clinic=='') grade = 2;
if (res >= 10 && res < lln && clinic=='') grade = 1;
   // Hemoglobin increased
if (res > uln && res <= (uln+2)) grade = 1;
if (res > (uln+2) && res <= (uln+4)) grade = 2;
if (res > (uln+4)) grade = 3;
if (isEmpty(uln) && isEmpty(lln)) grade = 'NA'};

// PLATELETS
    // Platelet count decreased
if (test == 'Platelets'){
if (res < 25) grade = 4;
if (res >= 25 && res < 50) grade = 3;
if (res >= 50 && res < 75) grade = 2;
if (res >= 75 && res < lln) grade = 1;
if (res >= lln && res <= uln) grade = 0;
if (res > uln) grade = 'NA';};

// NEUTROPHILS
    // Neutrophil count decreased
if (test == 'Neutrophils'){
if (res < 0.5) grade = 4;
if (res >= 0.5 && res < 1) grade = 3;
if (res >= 1 && res < 1.5) grade = 2;
if (res >= 1.5 && res < lln) grade = 1;
if (res >= lln && res <= uln) grade = 0;
if (res > uln) grade = 'NA';};


// EOSINOPHILS
if (test == 'Eosinophils') grade = 'NA';


// BASOPHILS
if (test == 'Basophils') grade = 'NA';


// LYMPHOCYTES
if (test == 'Lymphocytes'){
if (res >= lln && res <= uln) grade = 0;
    // Lymphocyte count decreased
if (res < 0.2) grade = 4;
if (res >= 0.2 && res < 0.5) grade = 3;
if (res >= 0.5 && res < 0.8) grade = 2;
if (res >= 0.8 && res < lln) grade = 1;
    // Lymphocyte count increased
if (res > 4 && res <= 20) grade = 2;
if (res > 20) grade = 3;
if (isEmpty(uln) && isEmpty(lln)) grade = 'NA'};


// MONOCYTES
if (test == 'Monocytes') grade = 'NA';


// SODIUM
if (test == 'Sodium'){
if (res >= lln && res <= uln) grade = 0;
    // Hyponatremia
if ((res < 120 && clinic=='') || clinic=='8') grade = 4;
if (res >= 120 && res < 130 && clinic=='') grade = 3;
if (res >= 130 && res < lln && clinic=='') grade = 1;
    // Hypernatremia
if ((res > 160 && clinic=='') || clinic=='8') grade = 4;
if ((res > 155 && res <= 160 && clinic=='') || clinic=='3') grade = 3;
if (res > 150 && res <= 155 && clinic=='') grade = 2;
if (res > uln && res <= 150 && clinic=='') grade = 1;
if (isEmpty(uln) && isEmpty(lln) && isEmpty(clinic)) grade = 'NA'};


// POTASSIUM
if (test == 'Potassium'){
if (res >= lln && res <= uln) grade = 0;
    // Hypokalemia
if ((res < 2.5 && clinic=='') || clinic=='8') grade = 4;
if ((res >= 2.5 && res < 3 && clinic=='') || clinic=='3') grade = 3;
if (clinic=='1' || clinic=='4') grade = 2;
if (res >= 3 && res < lln && clinic=='') grade = 1;
    // Hyperkalemia
if ((res > 7 && clinic=='') || clinic=='8') grade = 4;
if ((res > 6 && res <= 7 && clinic=='') || clinic=='3') grade = 3;
if (res > 5.5 && res <= 6 && clinic=='') grade = 2;
if (res > uln && res <= 5.5 && clinic=='') grade = 1;
if (isEmpty(uln) && isEmpty(lln)) grade = 'NA'};


// CHLORIDE
if (test == 'Chloride') grade = 'NA';


// GLUCOSE
if (test == 'Glucose'){
if (res >= lln && res <= uln) grade = 0;
    // Hypoglycemia
if ((res < 1.7) || clinic=='8' || clinic=='7') grade = 4;
if (res >= 1.7 && res < 2.2 && clinic=='') grade = 3;
if (res >= 2.2 && res < 3 && clinic=='') grade = 2;
if (res >= 3 && res < lln && clinic=='') grade = 1;
    // Hyperglycemia
if (res > 27.8 || clinic=='8') grade = 4;
if ((res > 13.9 && res <= 27.8 && clinic=='') || clinic=='3') grade = 3;
if (res > 8.9 && res <= 13.9 && clinic=='') grade = 2;
if (res > uln && res <= 8.9 && clinic=='') grade = 1;
if (isEmpty(uln) && isEmpty(lln) && isEmpty(clinic)) grade = 'NA'};


// CALCIUM
if (test == 'Calcium'){
if (res >= lln && res <= uln) grade = 0;
    // Hypocalcemia
if ((res < 1.5) || clinic=='8') grade = 4; 
if ((res >= 1.5 && res < 1.75 && clinic=='') || clinic=='3') grade = 3;
if ((res >= 1.75 && res < 2 && clinic=='') || clinic=='1') grade = 2;
if (res >= 2 && res < lln && clinic=='') grade = 1;
    // Hypercalcemia
if ((res > 3.4) || clinic=='8') grade = 4;
if ((res > 3.1 && res <= 3.4 && clinic=='') || clinic=='3') grade = 3;
if ((res > 2.9 && res <= 3.1 && clinic=='') || clinic=='1') grade = 2;
if (res > uln && res <= 2.9 && clinic=='') grade = 1;
if (isEmpty(uln) && isEmpty(lln) && isEmpty(clinic)) grade = 'NA'};


// PHOSPHORUS
if (test == 'Phosphorus') grade = 'NA';


// URIC ACID
    // Hyperuricemia
if (test == 'Uric acid'){
if (res > 590 || clinic=='8') grade = 4;
if (res > uln && res <= 590 && clinic=='6') grade = 3;
if (res > uln && res <= 590 && clinic=='5') grade = 1;
if (res < lln) grade = 'NA';
if (isEmpty(uln) && isEmpty(lln)) grade = 'NA'};


// MAGNESIUM
if (test == 'Magnesium'){
if (res >= lln && res <= uln) grade = 0;
    // Hypomagnesemia
if (res < 0.3 || clinic=='8') grade = 4;
if (res >= 0.3 && res < 0.4 && clinic=='') grade = 3;
if (res >= 0.4 && res < 0.5 && clinic=='') grade = 2;
if (res >= 0.5 && res < lln && clinic=='') grade = 1;
    // Hypermagnesemia
if (res > 3.3 || clinic=='8') grade = 4;
if (res > 1.23 && res <= 3.3 && clinic=='') grade = 3;
if (res > uln && res <= 1.23 && clinic=='') grade = 1;
if (isEmpty(uln) && isEmpty(lln) && isEmpty(clinic)) grade = 'NA'};


// ALKALINE PHOSPHATASE (PAL)
if (test == 'Alkaline phosphatase'){
if (res >= lln && res <= uln) grade = 0;
if (res < lln) grade = 'NA';
    // Alkaline phosphatase increased
if (res > (20*uln)) grade = 4;
if (res > (5*uln) && res <= (20*uln)) grade = 3;
if (res > (2.5*uln) && res <= (5*uln)) grade = 2;
if (res > uln && res <= (2.5*uln)) grade = 1;
if (isEmpty(uln) && isEmpty(lln)) grade = 'NA'};


// ASPARTATE AMINOTRANSFERASE (ASAT)
if (test == 'Aspartate aminotransferase (ASAT)'){
if (res >= lln && res <= uln) grade = 0;
if (res < lln) grade = 'NA';
    // Aspartate aminotransferase increased
if (res > (20*uln)) grade = 4;
if (res > (5*uln) && res <= (20*uln)) grade = 3;
if (res > (3*uln) && res <= (5*uln)) grade = 2;
if (res > uln && res <= (3*uln)) grade = 1;
if (isEmpty(uln) && isEmpty(lln)) grade = 'NA'};


// ALANINE AMINOTRANSFERASE (ALAT]
if (test == 'Alanine aminotransferase (ALAT)'){
if (res >= lln && res <= uln) grade = 0;
if (res < lln) grade = 'NA';
    // Alanine aminotransferase increased
if (res > (20*uln)) grade = 4;
if (res > (5*uln) && res <= (20*uln)) grade = 3;
if (res > (3*uln) && res <= (5*uln)) grade = 2;
if (res > uln && res <= (3*uln)) grade = 1;
if (isEmpty(uln) && isEmpty(lln)) grade = 'NA'};


// TOTAL BILIRUBIN
if (test == 'Total bilirubin'){
if (res >= lln && res <= uln) grade = 0;
if (res < lln) grade = 'NA';
    // Blood bilirubin increased
if (res > (10*uln)) grade = 4;
if (res > (3*uln) && res <=(10*uln)) grade = 3;
if (res > (1.5*uln) && res <= (3*uln)) grade = 2;
if (res > uln && res <= (1.5*uln)) grade = 1
if (isEmpty(uln) && isEmpty(lln)) grade = 'NA'};


// ALBUMIN
if (test == 'Albumin'){
if (res >= lln && res <= uln) grade = 0;
if (res > uln) grade = 'NA';
    // Hypoalbuminemia
if (res < lln && clinic=='8') grade = 4;
if (res < 20 && clinic=='') grade = 3;
if (res >= 20 && res < 30 && clinic=='') grade = 2;
if (res >= 30 && res < lln && clinic=='') grade = 1;};


// LACTATE DESHYDROGENASE (LDH)
if (test == 'Lactate deshydrogenase (LDH)') grade = 'NA';


// TOTAL PROTEIN
if (test == 'Total protein') grade = 'NA';


// PT (INR)
if (test == 'PT (INR)'){
if (res >= lln && res <= uln) grade = 0;
if (res < lln) grade = 'NA';
    // INR increased
if (res > (2.5*uln)) grade = 3;
if (res > (1.5*uln) && res <= (2.5*uln)) grade = 2;
if (res > uln && res <= (1.5*uln)) grade = 1;
if (isEmpty(uln) && isEmpty(lln)) grade = 'NA'};


// ACTIVATED PARTIAL THROMBOPLASTIN TIME
if (test == 'aPTT'){
if (res >= lln && res <= uln) grade = 0;
if (res < lln) grade = 'NA';
    // Activated partial thromboplastin time prolonged
if ((res > (2.5*uln)) || clinic=='9') grade = 3;
if (res > (1.5*uln) && res <= (2.5*uln) && clinic=='') grade = 2;
if (res > uln && res <= (1.5*uln) && clinic=='') grade = 1;
if (isEmpty(uln) && isEmpty(lln) && isEmpty(clinic)) grade = 'NA'};


// TOTAL TRIIODOTHYRONINE (T3)
if (test == 'Free triiodothyronine (FT3)') grade = 'NA';


// FREE TYROXINE (T4)
if (test == 'Free tyroxine (FT4)') grade = 'NA';


// THYROID STIMULATING HORMONE (TSH)
if (test == 'Thyroid stimulating hormone (TSH)') grade = 'NA';

// CREATININE
if (test == 'Creatinine'){
if (res >= lln && res <= uln) grade = 0;
if (res < lln) grade = 'NA';
    // Creatinine increased
if (res > (6*uln)) grade = 4;
if (res > (3*uln) && res <=(6*uln)) grade = 3;
if (res > (1.5*uln) && res <= (3*uln)) grade = 2;
if (res > uln && res <= (1.5*uln)) grade = 1;
if (isEmpty(uln) && isEmpty(lln)) grade = 'NA'};

// CREATININE CLEARANCE)
if (test == 'Creatinine clearance (mesured or calculated)') grade = 'NA';

// BLOOD UREA NITROGEN
if (test == 'Blood urea nitrogen') grade = 'NA' ;
else "";

## F13-End of treatment summary of care 
### Documentation 

<table style='width:100%;'>
<tr>
<th style='width:50px; text-align:center;'><strong>Sas</strong></th>
<th style='width:600px; text-align:center;'><strong>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;Label de la Question&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;</strong></th>
